<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пошлый.html>по́шлый</a> (1168)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пошьлъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pošĭlŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ancient, primordial, former, usual</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пошлый.html>по́шлый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">póšlyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пошле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пошле́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>vulgar</li>
<li>commonplace, trivial, banal, trite</li></ol>

***пощечина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пощечина.html>пощёчина</a> (10165)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щека́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščeká</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cheek</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ина</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">poezja</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">poetry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэзия.html>поэ́зия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poézija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэзия.html>поэ́зии</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>) (<i>no plural</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>poetry</li>
<li>charm, elegance, romantic appeal of something
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точность.html>то́чность</a> — <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поэзия.html>поэ́зия</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наука.html>нау́ки</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tóčnostʹ — <b>poézija</b> naúki.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Accuracy is the charm of science.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">poetry</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стихотворство</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stixotvorstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стихотворчество</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stixotvorčestvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">версифика́ция</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">versifikácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>pejorative</i>)</li></ul>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">charm, elegance, romantic appeal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:романтика.html>романтика</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">romantika</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поэма.html>поэ́ма</a> (7493)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэма.html>поэ́ма</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poéma</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэма.html>поэ́мы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэма.html>поэ́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэма.html>поэ́м</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>poem <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">large poem</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***поэтесса.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поэтесса.html>поэте́сса</a> (17563)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэтесса.html>поэте́сса</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poetɛ́ssa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэтесса.html>поэте́ссы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэтесса.html>поэте́ссы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэтесса.html>поэте́сс</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэт.html>поэ́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>poetess, woman poet</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Sometimes interpreted as not quite equal to the masculine <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэт.html>поэ́т</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poét</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Several famous female Russian poets, notably <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anna_Akhmatova" class="extiw" title="w:Anna Akhmatova">Anna Akhmatova</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marina_Tsvetaeva" class="extiw" title="w:Marina Tsvetaeva">Marina Tsvetaeva</a>, insisted on being called <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэт.html>поэ́т</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poét</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and regarded the term <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэтесса.html>поэте́сса</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poetɛ́ssa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> as insulting.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэт.html>поэ́т</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poét</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэма.html>поэ́ма</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poéma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

<p>Univerbation of the preposition <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">according to</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тому</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">étomu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, dative singular of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">étot</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***появиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:появиться.html>появи́ться</a> (333)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явиться.html>яви́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">javítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:появиться.html>появи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pojavítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:появляться.html>появля́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to appear, to show up, to emerge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:луна.html>луна́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:появиться.html>появи́лась</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Luná <b>pojavílasʹ</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The moon is out.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:солнце.html>со́лнце</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:появиться.html>появи́лось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:увидеть.html>уви́дели</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:радуга.html>ра́дугу</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Sólnce <b>pojavílosʹ</b> pósle doždjá i my uvídeli rádugu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The sun came out after the rain, and we saw a rainbow.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:вить.html>ви́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pȍjāsъ</i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пояс.html>по́яс</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pójas</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пояс.html>по́яса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пояс.html>пояса́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пояс.html>поясо́в</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пояснивший.html>поясни́вший</a> (2395)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пояснивший.html>поясни́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pojasnívšij</span>)
</p>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>пра<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ба.html>ба́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>буш<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>

***правда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>правда</a> (204)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">правьда</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pravĭda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pravьda</i>, derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pravъ</i> (compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">právyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) plus an unclear suffix. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>пра́вда</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">právda</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">truth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">пра́ўда</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">práŭda</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">truth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">правьда</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pravĭda</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">justice, truth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>пра́вда</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">právda</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">justice, truth, livestock capital</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">пра̑вда</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">justice, truth, controversial matter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">prȃvda</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">pravda</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">truth</span><span title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">pravda</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>пра́вда</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">právda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>пра́вды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>пра́вды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>пра́вд</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>truth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> «<b><a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>пра́вде</a></b>» <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:известие.html>изве́стий</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:известие.html>изве́стиях</a>» <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>пра́вды</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V “<b>Právde</b>” net izvéstij, a v “Izvéstijax” net <b>právdy</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">In <i>Pravda</i> there is no news, and in <i>Izvestia</i> there is no <b>truth</b>. (a familiar pun)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>По</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>пра́вде</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случайно.html>случа́йно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сутки.html>су́тки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:принять.html>при́нял</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лекарство.html>лека́рства</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Po <b>právde</b> skazátʹ, ja slučájno za sútki ne prínjal lekárstva.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">To tell (you) the <b>truth</b>, by accident, I didn't take my medicine for 24 hours.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>Ну</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>пра́вда</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nu <b>právda</b> že?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Really? (in a rhetorical sense)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>пра́вде</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говоря́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po <b>právde</b> govorjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tell <b>the truth</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>пра́в</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a></b>
